I would like to give it a thumbs up first. I am honored to feel the hotel's full hospitality in advance and get a free room upgrade.

The first impression when entering the door is that the hotel lobby is very spacious and grand.

After check-in, welcome fruit and ice cola and Sprite are given for free. The breakfast restaurant is large and classy, ‚Äã‚Äãwith a rich variety of breakfasts. It seems that there are few grilled shrimps and grilled fish. There are many people eating and the taste is very good.

I usually book hotels for the swimming pool, but this hotel did not specifically mark the swimming pool on Ctrip. After various comparisons, it was found that there was actually one. It is recommended to add highlights. I took the children to swim twice in the morning and evening for one day. There were several children swimming in the evening, and there were almost no people swimming in the morning. The experience was very good.

The Dragon Tower can be seen opposite the room, and there is a bright halo at night.

The room is very clean, with a shower and a bathtub, and the quality of the bathrobe is very thick inside and outside. I ordered takeout twice, and there was a robot to deliver the food. I just sat in the room and waited for the meal, which was convenient and fast.

I opened the sliding window, but didn't use the air conditioner. The door was thick, and it was quiet at night. The mattress was moderately hard and soft, and the children and adults slept well. Next to it is Wanda Mall, but I only ordered takeout and didn't go shopping.

It's about 9 minutes from the subway entrance to the provincial museum, which is convenient.

The only drawback is that I can charge my mobile phone with the multi-sided plug on the bedside table at night, but when I left the hotel in the morning, I found that I couldn't charge my two mobile phones after charging for half a day. I suspect that I didn't press a key on the panel at the bedside during the day, and the mobile phone ran out of power quickly that day. It was a mistake.

Overall, it's a five-star rating, and the experience of both children and adults is very good. It is recommended to stay. The price for May Day is a bit expensive for reference.
